 Pakistan Prime Minister Imran Khan claimed during the foundation stone of Kartarpur Corridor on Wednesday that both India and Pakistan are nuclear armed countries
 imran ne kaha- isliye donon deshon ke bich kisi tarah ke yuddh ke bare main sochna morrkhtaa se bharaa kaa kaam he
 Through this statement, Imran Khan argued that since both countries are armed with nuclear weapons, both countries are equal in strategic power and in the event of war both countries are bound to be destroyed
 haalanki donon deshon kii vaastavik sthiti or maujuuda daur main yuddh ke prachlit siddhanton kii maane to bharat or pakistan ke bich yuddh main agar newclear hathiyaaron kaa istemaal hota he to jahaan bharat ko ek badi kshati pahunchane kii ashanka he vahiin ek baat tay he ki duniya ke nakshe se pakistan puri tarah gaayab ho jayega
 Dr
 Soumyajit Ray, Assistant Professor at Jawaharlal Nehru University School of International Studies and who works in the field of National Security, explains this in detail
 saumyajit re ke mutabik kai dashak se bhartiya sena ke top brass kaa daawa he ki pakistan dwaara newclear hathiyaaron ke saath kisi dussahas ko munhtod jawaab dene kaa samyarth bharat main he
 According to this claim, if Pakistan tries to launch any kind of nuclear attack on India, where India can clear the entire map of the earth from thwarting that attack to counter attack
 nehru indira rahe naakaam, kya PM Modi banaaenge bharat ko P-6?lihaaja, imran khan kaa daawa sachai se koso dur he
 Whether or not nuclear weapons are used in the event of war between India and Pakistan and if the war is fought entirely with conventional weapons, one thing is clear that the outcome of the war will be in India's favor
 darasal imran khan ne apni yah daleel dashakon pehle america or uasasar (maujuuda rus) ke bich sheet yuddh ke dauraan aae yuddh ke siddhant MAD (mutually Assured Destruction) par aadhaarit he
 This theory says that if two countries armed with nuclear weapons use nuclear weapons during war, then life will end in both the countries
 haalanki imran khan ne is siddhant ko or is siddhant par sheet yuddh ke vakt uthe tamaam pakshon ko nazarandaaj kar diya
 In this theory, one side believes that when there exists a big geographical and numerical difference between the two countries, then in case of nuclear war, where big countries in geography and population remain in the treaty of not attacking first and it will be attacked
 In this situation he may have to bear a heavy loss
 jeenyu ke skool of international studies ke ek anya associat professor dow
 Rajan Kumar said that after World War II and during the Cold War, the USSR had a stock of nuclear weapons more than the US
 iske baavjood sheet yuddh ke dashakon ke dauraan apni arthvyavastha, loktantric saamaajik parivesh or bhugol ke chalate america haaavee rahaa
 indo-pak trade will be 6 times, just turn from terrorism to Imran! Professor Rajan Kumar cites another example, saying that at present, both America and Russia are intervening in Syria
 donon hi desh newclear hathiyaaron se las hai iske baavjood paaramparik hathiyaaron ke sahare donon desh syria main apni shakti kaa parichay de rahe hai
 Both, America and Russia, despite being a nuclear armed country, do not consider the possibility of war as foolishness or insanity
 in tathyon ko aadhaar maanate hue sawaal uthta he ki aakhir imran khan ne yuddh kii soch rakhane waalon ko murkh athwa pagal kyon kaha? is sawaal par dow
 Saumyajit Ray says that the biggest drawback of democracy is that through this, one can occupy the top post of a country
 jahaan pakistan banane ke baad se hi pakistan kii sena or pakistan kii loktantric partiyon ke bich varchasv kii ladaai hi he
 Apart from these, fundamentalist institutions in Pakistan have been doing politics of pressure on army and political parties
 haalanki is ladaai main hameshaa pakistan kii sena kaa palada baari rahaa or kattarpanthi shaktiyaan sena ke samarthan main raheen
 But democratic parties have always proved a headache for him
 pakistan ke itihaas main yah pehla mauka he jab pakistani sena ne ek kattarpanthi raajnneetik dal ko na sirf khadaa karne main safalataa pai balki us raajnneetik dal ko satta par asin bhi kar diya
 Therefore, Imran Khan's statement is the face of Pakistani fundamentalism which is working to advance the policies of the army and fundamentalist institutions

 Nuclear power talks, which began in 2010, have stagnated since the Fukushima nuclear accident in March 2011
 antim vaarta november 2010 main hui thi
 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh and his Japanese counterpart Shinzo Abe decided in May to instruct their officials in Tokyo to expedite negotiations to expedite cooperation in the peaceful use of nuclear energy

 india-japan civil nuclear agreements are very important for India struggling with a huge energy shortage, as Japanese companies have a monopoly on the supply of reactor vessels, an important component of civil nuclear plants, and the absence of such agreements makes these companies These components will not be able to be supplied to French and American companies that have received orders for nuclear plants in India
 tippaniyan In a joint statement issued after the talks, the two sides reiterated that bilateral cooperation in the civil nuclear energy sector is important and the two sides also welcomed the fact that the nuclear power workforce met earlier this month
 donon netaaon ke bich parmaanu urja nitiyon par bhi charchaa hui

 The results of Betul Lok Sabha seat of Madhya Pradesh have been announced
 yahaan se bijepi ke durga das didi ne jeet hasil kii he
 He defeated Ramu Tekam of Congress by 360241 votes
 kab or kitni hui votingis seat par paanchaven charan main 6 april ko voting hui thi, jisamen kshetra ke kul 1734849 votaron main se 78
 20 percent exercised their franchise
 ye the ummidavaaris baar yahaan se 9 pratyaashee hai
 The Bharatiya Janata Party fielded Durga Das DD Uike, Congress Party Ramu Tekam, Bahujan Samaj Party, Ashok Bhalvi, Bahujan Mukti Party Pushpa Marscole, All India Gondwana Party Pushpa Shailendra Pendam and Gondwana Ganatantra Party fielded Bisram Uike

 SOCIAL TANA-BANABATUL District is located in the south of Madhya Pradesh
 iskaa apana ek dharmik or aitihaasik mahatv he
 The Marathas and the British ruled here for a long time
 baitool jila narmada sambhag ke antargat aata tha
 According to the 2011 census, Betul has a population of 24 lakh 59 thousand 626
 yahaan kii 81
 68 percent of the population in rural areas and 18
 32 fisadi aabaadi shahari kshetra main rahati he
 40 here
 56 fisadi aabaadi anusuchit janajati ke logon kii he or 11
 28 percent of the population belongs to scheduled castes
 chunaav ayog ke aankade ke mutabik 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav main yahaan par 16 lakh 7 hajaar 822 matadaata the
 Of these, 7 lakh 70 thousand 987 were female voters and 8 lakh 36 thousand 835 male voters
 saal 2014 ke chunaav main is seat par 65
 The turnout was 16 percent
 raajnneetik prishthbhumibaitool loksabhaa seat par pehla chunaav 1951 main hua
 Congress won the first Lok Sabha election
 saal 1967 or 1971 ke chunaav main bhi is seat par congress ne jeet hasil kii thi
 In the 1977 elections, this seat was passed by the Congress and the Bharatiya Lok Dal had won here for the first time
 haalanki saal 1980 main congress ne yahaan par vaapasi kii thi or gupran ajam yahaan ke saansad bane the
 The Congress also won its next election in 1984
 bijepi ne pehali baar yahaan par jeet 1989 main hasil kii
 Arif Baig defeated bjp's Aslam Sherkhan to give BJP its first victory here

 inputah bhashaa In Chhattisgarh, the word Dalit has been banned in government and non-government records
 sarkaar ne baqayada aadesh jari kar dalit ke sthaan par jati kaa ullekh karne kaa nirdesh diya he
 The order, issued just before the assembly elections in the state, was termed by Congress as part of the social engineering of Chief Minister Raman Singh
 party kaa daawa he ki yah circular nahin balki ek shigupha he
 Government issued circular a few months before the assembly elections in Chhattisgarh, the state government has issued this circular and tried to help a large community of scheduled castes
 centre sarkaar ke disha-nirdeshon kaa hawala dete hue rajya sarkaar ne sabhi sarkari dastavejon main dalit shabd ke istemaal par roak laga di he
 The General Administration Department of Chhattisgarh Government, while directing all the government departments of the state, has said that this word is not in the constitution
 isliye iskaa prayog naa ho
 In the era of joint Madhya Pradesh before the formation of the state, the then government issued a notification on February 10, 1982 and banned the word Harijan
 is shabd ke istemaal par sajaa kaa bhi praavdhaan kiya gaya, lekin dalit shabd ke prayog par kitni sajaa kaa praavdhaan hoga yah spasht nahin he
 It is said that after the instructions of Chief Minister Raman Singh, the General Administration Department has issued this circular and gave directions to all departments
 iske ulanghan par sajaa ke praavdhaan par vichaar kiya ja rahaa he
 According to Chief Minister Raman Singh, Congress never gave the respect to Dalits
 wo bijepi ke satta main aane ke baad unki party de rahi he
 He said that this society is hurt by the word Dalit
 isliye is par pabandi lagaai gai he
 This will further increase the respect of the Scheduled Castes
 anusuchit jati kii aabaadi badhichhattisgarhmen anusuchit jati varg kii aabaadi varsh 2011 ke janaganana ke lihaaj se 12 fisadi thi
 It is estimated that in 2018 it has increased by more than 3%
 rajya main anusuchit jati varg ke liye kul 90 main se 10 siten arakshit hai
 Of this, BJP holds 9 seats
 jabaki ek seat par congress kaa kabja he
 Therefore, by banning the use of the word Dalit, the BJP government of the state is making every effort to keep this large section in its camp
 rajya kii bijepi sarkaar ne anusuchit jati varg ke liye kai kalyankari yojanaayen barason se jari he, lekin yah varg mahasoos karata tha ki sarkari dastavejon main dalit shabd unke sammaan kaa hanan karata tha
 So throw this word out and throw it out
 siem raman sinhane apane tisare kaarykaal ke antim daur main dalit shabd ko baahar kaa rasta dikhaakar is varg ko bijepi ke bheetar banaae rakhane ke liye fouran aadesh jari kar diya
 The Congress said, this votebank politics, the decision of the BJP government is not acceptable to the Congress
 uskaa maananaa he ki raman singh kii yah shigufe vaali ek chaal he, jo vot bank ke khatir chali gai he
 According to the party, the justification for this decision, taken a few days before the assembly elections, is only to give vent to vote bank politics
 congress upaadhyaksh ramesh varlini ke mutabik bijepi ne yah nayaa shigupha choda he
 He alleged that in 15 years, BJP has never seen respect for the Scheduled Castes
 abhi vidhansabha chunaav aa gaya to party is varg ke sammaan ko lekar chintit ho rahi he
 He said that this is Raman Singh's thoughtful social engineering, but BJP will not benefit from it
 chhattisgarh main isi saal oktober-november maah main hone vaale vidhansabha chunaav kii taiyaariyon ko lekar bijepi or congress aamane-saamne he
 Along with activating the activists, the parties have also been able to activate the people of caste, community and religion, whose class of votes fall in their baggage
 bihar ko lekar gujarat ke mukhyamantri narendra modi dwaara die bayaan se naaraaz bihar ke mukhyamantri nitish kumaar ne palatwaar karte hue modi ko apana ghar sanbhaalane kii salaah di or kaha ki vah (modi) pehle apana daaman dekhen
 At the same time, Nitish advised Modi not to comment on Bihar and said that Bihar is moving forward on the path of development while fighting its weaknesses
 nitish ne yah bhi kaha ki ham dusron par tippanee nahin karte, so, koi or bhi bihar par tippanee na kare to acha hoga
 It is noteworthy that in his address on Sunday during the concluding session of the two-day meeting of the BJP executive held in Rajkot, Modi said that the state fell behind due to caste politics by the leaders of Bihar
 isi bayaan ko lekar bihar main sattashin janata dal (united) or vipakshi dal rashtriya janata dal ne modi kii khinchaai kii thi
 Member of Bihar Legislative Council and JD (U) State Spokesperson Neeraj Kumar said that Modi is still struggling with his party and a lot of internal crises in Gujarat, so in this case he is not expressing his heart, but somewhere But eyes are targeting somewhere
 niraj kaa kahana tha ki ki aisi baat kehane se purv modi ko dhyaan rakhana chahie ki yahaan unki party bhi sarkaar main shaamil he
 Neeraj said that Gujarat inherited the infrastructure and most of Bihar was affected by floods and drought, but despite that due to the efficiency of the Chief Minister of the state, Nitish Kumar, great achievements were made here
 niraj ne kaha ki desh ke aarthik aankadon ne sabit kar diya he ki bihar jaisaa bimaaru rajya vikaas dar or prati vyakti aay ke maamle main gujarat se bahut aage he or bihar kaa jo gauravpurn itihaas purv main rahaa he, yah usee disha main badhata hua kadam he
 According to the JD (U) state spokesperson, the growth rate achieved in Bihar despite these adverse conditions is the result of our actions in the field of infrastructure
 vittiya prabandhan kii badaulat ham ise vikaas ke maarg par aage lekar chal rahe hai
 He said that caste bonds have been broken in Bihar
 yahaan 115 narsanhaar hue the, jo ab band hue hai tathaa yahaan saamaajik samarasata evam sampradayik sauhaard kaa maahaul bana he, vah kuch logon ko raas nahin aa rahaa he
 Neeraj said that Nitish often says that social harmony and communal harmony are our capital and the human labor of 10 crore people of Bihar, due to which Bihar is developing and so is Modi's party in power in Bihar
 People also say
 unhone kaha ki log bayaanbaji karte rahete hai, parantu mukhyamantri karm main vishwaas rakhte hai, or bihar jaise bimaaru rajya ko viksit pradesh kii disha main le jane kii koshish kar rahe hai, yah baat desh or duniya kabool kar rahi he
 The comments modi ke is bayaan ko bihar main pratibandhit jaateey sanghathan brahmeshwar mukhiya kii hatya or uske baad unke samarthakon dwaara todphod or aagjanee kii ghatnaon se jodakar dekhe jane ke bare main poochne par niraj ne kaha ki sthiti kaa moolyankan kiya jaae to agar us din police karrwai karti to gaanvon main badi mushkil se sthapit saamaajik sauhaard bighad saktaa tha
 He said that the Bihar government acted with restraint and also decided that those who had caused a fuss during that time would be identified and made a speedy trial, so that no one could dare in future
 iske saath hi nitish ne modi ko bihar par tippanee na karne kii salaah dete hue kaha ki bihar apni kamajoriyon se ladate hue vikaas kii raah par aage bad rahaa he
 Nitish also said that we do not comment on others, so if no one else comments on Bihar, it will be good
 ullekhneey he ki rajkot main hui bhaajapa kaaryakarini kii do-divasiy baithak ke samaapan satr ke dauraan ravivaar ko apane sambodhan main modi ne kaha tha ki bihar ke netaaon dwaara jatigat raajnneeti kiye jane ke kaaran yah pradesh pichad gaya
 Modi was pulled by the ruling Janata Dal (united) and opposition party Rashtriya Janata Dal in Bihar for this statement
 bihar vidhanparishad ke sadsy or jad (you) ke pradesh pravaktaa niraj kumaar ne kaha ki modi abhi apni party or gujarat ke bahut saare andruni sankaton se jujh rahe hai, so, aise main vah apane man ke bhav pragat nahin kar rahe hai, balki kahin par nigahen, kahin par nishaanaa laga rahe hai
 Neeraj said that before saying such a thing, Modi should take care that his party is also included in the government here
 niraj ne kaha ki gujarat ko aadharbhoot sanrachana viraasat main mili or bihar kaa adhikansh hissaa baadh or sukhaad se prabhavit rahaa, parantu uske baavjood pradesh ke mukhyamantri nitish kumaar kii kaarykushalta ke boote yahaan badi uplabdhiyaan hasil kii gayi
 Neeraj said that the economic data of the country has proved that a sick state like Bihar is far ahead of Gujarat in terms of growth rate and per capita income, and the glorious history of Bihar in the past, it is a step in the same direction
 is
 jad (you) ke pradesh pravaktaa ke mutabik bihar main in pratikul paristhitiyon ke baavjood jo vikaas dar hasil hui he, vah aadharbhoot sanrachana ke kshetra main hamaare kaaryon kaa nateeja he
 Thanks to financial management, we are taking it forward on the path of development
 unhone kaha ki bihar main jatigat bandhan toote hai
 There were 115 massacres here, which are now closed and there has been an atmosphere of social harmony and communal harmony, some people do not like it
 niraj ne kaha ki nitish aksar kaha karte hai ki saamaajik samarasata evam sampradayik sauhaard hamaari puunji hai or bihar kii 10 karod janata kaa maanav shram he, jisaki badaulat bihar vikaas kar rahaa he or aisa hi bihar main satta main shaamil modi ji kii party bhaajapa ke log bhi kehete hai

 tippaniyan Asked about Modi's statement about the murder of the banned caste organization Brahmeshwar Mukhiya in Bihar and then his supporters linked to the incidents of sabotage and arson, Neeraj said that if the situation is evaluated, the police would have taken action that day So the social harmony established in the villages with great difficulty could have deteriorated
